-- specification !(state = net &  X ( F (state = http &  X ( F state = DB))))  is false
-- as demonstrated by the following execution sequence
Trace Description: LTL Counterexample 
Trace Type: Counterexample 
  -> State: 1.1 <-
    state = net
    other = FALSE
  -> Input: 1.2 <-
    operation = read
  -> State: 1.2 <-
    state = http
  -> Input: 1.3 <-
    operation = write
  -> State: 1.3 <-
    state = DB
  -> Input: 1.4 <-
    operation = read
  -> State: 1.4 <-
    state = anon
  -> Input: 1.5 <-
  -- Loop starts here
  -> State: 1.5 <-
    state = pozzo
  -> Input: 1.6 <-
  -> State: 1.6 <-

-- as demonstrated by the following execution sequence
Trace Description: LTL Counterexample

    state = DB
    other = FALSE

    operation = read

  -> State: 2.4 <-

  -- Loop starts here
  -> State: 2.5 <-

  -> State: 2.6 <-
